<TITLE>EX-99.1</TITLE>

 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.1 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:13pt; font-family:ARIAL">Microsoft Cloud Strength Highlights Third Quarter Results </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><I>Commercial cloud annualized revenue run rate exceeds $10.0 billion; Windows 10 active on over 270&nbsp;million devices </I></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>REDMOND, Wash. &#151; April&nbsp;21, 2016 &#151;</B> Microsoft Corp. today announced the following results for the quarter ended March&nbsp;31,
2016: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Revenue was $20.5 billion GAAP, and $22.1 billion non-GAAP </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Operating income was $5.3 billion GAAP, and $6.8 billion non-GAAP </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Net income was $3.8 billion GAAP, and $5.0 billion non-GAAP </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Earnings per share was $0.47 GAAP, and $0.62 non-GAAP </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&#147;Organizations using digital technology to transform and drive new growth increasingly choose Microsoft as a partner,&#148; said Satya
Nadella, chief executive officer at Microsoft. &#147;As these organizations turn to us, we&#146;re seeing momentum across Microsoft&#146;s cloud services and with Windows 10.&#148; </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">The following table reconciles our financial results reported in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles (&#147;GAAP&#148;) to
non-GAAP financial results. Microsoft has provided this non-GAAP financial information to aid investors in better understanding the company&#146;s performance. All growth comparisons relate to the corresponding period in the last fiscal year.
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" WIDTH="100%" BORDER="0" STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" ALIGN="center">


<TR>
<TD WIDTH="93%"></TD>

dividends. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">This quarter&#146;s income tax expense included a catch-up adjustment to account for an expected increase in the full year
effective tax rate primarily due to the changing mix of revenue across geographies, as well as between cloud services and software licensing. As such, the GAAP and non-GAAP tax rates were 25% and 24%, respectively. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&#147;Our continued operational and financial discipline drove solid results this quarter,&#148; said Amy Hood, executive vice president and chief
financial officer at Microsoft. &#147;We remain focused on investing in our strategic priorities to drive long-term growth.&#148; </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Revenue in Productivity and Business Processes grew 1% (up 6% in constant currency) to $6.5 billion, with the following business highlights:

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Business Outlook </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Microsoft will provide forward-looking guidance in connection with this quarterly earnings announcement on its earnings conference call and
webcast. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Webcast Details </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT
 COLOR="#666666">Satya Nadella, chief executive officer, Amy Hood, executive vice president and chief financial officer, Frank Brod, chief accounting officer, John Seethoff, deputy general counsel and corporate secretary, and Chris Suh, general
manager of Investor Relations, will host a conference call and webcast at 2:30 p.m. Pacific time (5:30 p.m. Eastern time) today to discuss details of the company&#146;s performance for the quarter and certain forward-looking information. The session
may be accessed at http://www.microsoft.com/en-us/investor. The webcast will be available for replay through the close of business on April&nbsp;21, 2017. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT
 COLOR="#666666"><B>Adjusted Financial Results and non-GAAP Measures </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">During the third quarter of fiscal year 2016, GAAP revenue,
operating income, net income, and earnings per share include the net impact from revenue deferrals. For the third quarter of fiscal year 2015, GAAP operating income, net income, and earnings per share include charges related to integration and
restructuring expenses. These items are defined below. In addition to these financial results reported in accordance with GAAP, Microsoft has provided certain non-GAAP financial information to aid investors in better understanding the company&#146;s
performance. Presenting these non-GAAP measures gives additional insight into operational performance and helps clarify trends affecting the company&#146;s business. For comparability of reporting, management considers this information in
conjunction with GAAP amounts in evaluating business performance. These non-GAAP financial measures should not be considered as a substitute for, or superior to, the measures of financial performance prepared in accordance with GAAP. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Non-GAAP Definitions </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><I>Net Impact from Revenue Deferrals</I>. Microsoft recorded a net $1.5 billion revenue deferral during the three months ended March&nbsp;31,
2016, primarily related to Windows 10. </FONT></P>

<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><I>Integration and Restructuring Charges</I>. Integration and restructuring expenses were $190
million during the three months ended March&nbsp;31, 2015. Integration and restructuring expenses include employee severance expenses and costs associated with the consolidation of facilities and manufacturing operations related to restructuring
activities, and systems consolidation and other business integration expenses associated with the acquisition of Nokia&#146;s Devices and Services business. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Constant Currency </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Microsoft presents constant currency information to provide a non-GAAP framework for assessing how our underlying businesses performed excluding
the effect of foreign currency rate fluctuations. To present this information, current and comparative prior period non-GAAP results for entities reporting in currencies other than United States dollars are converted into United States dollars using
the average exchange rates from the comparative period rather than the actual exchange rates in effect during the respective periods. The non-GAAP financial measures presented below should not be considered as a substitute for, or superior to, the
measures of financial performance prepared in accordance with GAAP. All growth comparisons relate to the corresponding period in the last fiscal year. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:7%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Financial Performance Constant Currency Reconciliation </B></FONT></P>
